# Front Theme Implementation Guide

## Theme Overview

The front project uses a **Purple/Violet theme** (not blue) with the following
characteristics:

### Color Palette

```css
/* Primary Colors - Purple */
--primary-50: #faf5ff;
--primary-100: #f3e8ff;
--primary-200: #e9d5ff;
--primary-300: #d8b4fe;
--primary-400: #c084fc;
--primary-500: #a855f7;
--primary-600: #9333ea; /* Main primary color */
--primary-700: #7c3aed;
--primary-800: #6b21a8;
--primary-900: #581c87;

/* Secondary Colors - Gray */
--secondary-50: #fafafa; /* Background color */
--secondary-100: #f4f4f5;
--secondary-200: #e4e4e7;
--secondary-300: #d4d4d8;
--secondary-400: #a1a1aa;
--secondary-500: #71717a;
--secondary-600: #52525b;
--secondary-700: #3f3f46;
--secondary-800: #27272a;
--secondary-900: #18181b;
```

### Typography

- **Font Family**: Inter (with system font fallbacks)
- **Code Font**: JetBrains Mono, Fira Code

### Key Styling Features

1. **Gradient Backgrounds**: `linear-gradient(135deg, #faf5ff 0%, #e9d5ff 100%)`
2. **Card Hover Effects**: Shadow + translateY animation
3. **Button Shadows**: Purple-tinted shadows on primary buttons
4. **Custom Scrollbar**: Styled with gray colors
5. **Animations**: fade-in, slide-up, slide-fade-in/out

## Implementation Steps

### 1. Update Tailwind Configuration

Already updated in `tailwind.config.js` with:

- Purple color palette
- Inter font family
- Custom animations

### 2. Update Material-UI Theme

Already updated in `src/js/theme/theme.ts` with:

- Purple primary colors
- Gray secondary colors
- Inter typography
- Component overrides for buttons, cards, app bar

### 3. Update Global Styles

Already updated in `src/sass/tailwind.css` with:

- Olorin-specific utility classes
- Custom scrollbar
- Animation classes
- Focus and selection styles

### 4. Update Components

Need to update all components to use:

- Purple color scheme instead of blue
- `primary.main` (#9333ea) for main actions
- `secondary` colors for text and backgrounds
- Gradient backgrounds for hero sections
- Card hover effects with purple shadows

### 5. Add Fonts

- Inter font: Already included in `public/index.html`
- JetBrains Mono: Need to add for code blocks

## Component-Specific Changes

### Navigation Bar

- White background with border-bottom
- Purple active states
- Hover effects with purple tint

### Cards

- White background
- Rounded corners (12px)
- Hover: shadow + translateY(-4px)
- Transition animations

### Buttons

- Primary: Purple with shadow
- Hover: Darker purple + larger shadow
- Text transform: none (no uppercase)
- Font weight: 600

### Forms

- Border radius: 8px
- Focus: Purple border with shadow
- Gray borders in default state

### Material-UI sx Props

```javascript
sx={{
  backgroundColor: 'primary.main',  // #9333ea
  color: 'text.primary',  // #18181b
  '&:hover': {
    backgroundColor: 'primary.dark',  // #7c3aed
    boxShadow: '0 6px 16px rgba(147, 51, 234, 0.4)',
  }
}}
```
